 Sahitya Aaj Tak interacted with the writer-professor-urmila Shirish, a storyteller and writer associated with many social and literary organizations, along with the role of the judge in several national awards and awards committee
 anshah1
 Tell me about your childhood, education, and the process of being a writer? - My childhood has been spent in the very beautiful environment of the village, green fields, Palash forests, festivals colors, folk songs, hymns and songs The echoes are still echoing in my ears today
 vahaan ke logon ke saath jo rishta tha, vah atyant atmiyata se bharaa or antarang tha
 They have come into my stories as characters, but many still have to come
 ghar main padhane kaa maahaul tha
 The room was full of books
 bacchon kii patrikas, us samay kii sabhi patr-patrikas tathaa kitaaben mere aasapaas rahati thim
 When the girls with me used to play, i found myself in the middle of the books with them, those characters
 lekhak banane kii prakriya main do kahaniyon kaa prabhaav mujh par tha
 One 'victory of defeat', the other 'kabuliwala'
 in kahaniyon ne mujhe bahut zyaada prabhavit kiya tha
 Secondly, my Hindi teacher who gave a subject to write a story, then after reading my story, he said that you should write a story
 
 
 yahi mere lekhak banane kii prakriya he
 Literature has always been the best and favorite subject in my life
 jeene kii takat
 2
 aap apni kahaniyon ke liye paatr kahan se chunati hai? agar un paatro main se kisi sabase achche paatr ko chunane ko kaha jaae, to kise chunegi or kyon?- meri kahaniyon ke paatr mere aasapaas ke samaaj se, jivan se aate hai
 They sit inside me
 mujhase sawaal karte hai
 Inspire me to tell the story of my life
 sangharsh karte paatr meri kahaniyon main zyaadaatar aaye hai, kyonki sangharsh se jeeta hua manushya jivan main kabhi paraajay sweekaar nahin karata he
 There are a lot of characters from all the stories, but if you want to know about the best character then she is the 'girl' of the 'scream' story, who is a player, cool, easygoing
 
 
 lekin balaatkaar kii shikaar ho jaati he
 Then the events that occur in her life, the kind of atmosphere, tension, hatred she sees, endures
 
 
 achaanak ek din parivaar dekhtaa he ki vah scooter uthaakar punah khilne ke liye ja rahi he

 Do you consider any impact of gender discrimination in the field of writing? Have you ever felt something like this because of being a female writer? - i do not believe in gender at all in the field of writing, because even if i accept it, then many writers like Sharat Chandra, Jainendra Kumar, Leo Tolstoy are in front of me
 Come, who has expressed the woman's life very closely, sensitively in her creations
 rachanaatmak str par, chetana or bhavabodh ke str par main kabhi bhi is baat ko sweekaar nahin kar pai hoon, na maine kabhi yah mahasoos kiya he ki main stri lekhak hone ke kaaran kuch likhane main asamarth hoon
 i like to see myself as a writer
 haalaanki yah sawaal bhi uthaaya jaataa he ki swayan kaa bhoga or dekha yatharth zyaada pramanik hota he, magar isse bhi zyaada mahatvapurn baat hoti he ‚Äòparakaaya pravesh‚Äô kii

 If the accused says that he has been implicated under the conspiracy then the matter is different but if a DGP says that the victim is false then what will the police investigate the matter? The question here is that if the person on the position is rhetorical in this way, even if a crime It is not within the scope of, but it also comes under the purview of morality and etiquette given in the Constitution
 vahiin, centre sarkaar kii ore se iskaa virodh kiya gaya
